< text>
We love the Mayflower Market, our neighborhood corner store. Lefty, one of the owners, is so friendly, as is the rest of his family that runs the place. They have a good assortment of food, wine, snacks, fruit, and soft drinks. Plus they have a great deli. You can find almost everything you need, except for what you'd get at the meat counter, there. And they are open to feedback and suggestions.<//text>

<user_id>108476892568623540954<//user_id><name>Mark Casey</name><Time>1377511015045</Time><rating>4</rating>< Text>
This is a way better than average corner market.  Not only do they have all the usual convenience stuff -- snacks, candy, ice cream, etc. -- but they also have a pretty good selection of more grocery store stuff, including fruits and vegetables.  The guys who run the place are professional and fast.  It's usually easy to find parking somewhere on Jackson street.< /Text>

He was able to return with a camera the next night and give us a very comprehensive review of the problem - roots had grown into the pipes, and he was able to pinpoint exactly where this had occurred in our yard, despite our not having a clean-out pipe.

He also showed us a future problem we will have (roots growing through the pipes, but under the street) that will require a different, more expensive plumber, but he assured us we didn't need that yet.

<Review>Came here because a friend recommended this place and it was definitely the right choice. It is all you can eat meats and unlimited buffet of sides. The sides had a lot of variety like soups, salad, etc.

This is a lot different from a typical buffet style. The servers actually come out with different types of meat and cut it for you on the spot. However, I did get full a lot quicker since I had to wait for the meats to come. The meats were all so good. I normally don't like pineapples but the ones they had, which is smoked in cinnamon, was sooo good.

They also give free flans if it is someone's birthday. The flan was so soft and delicious. Service was also very good. They also have a parking lot next to it or you can park on the streets!

Overall, give this place a try! Definitely worth the price and great experience.< /Review><user_name>Maria Bailey</user_name>< response>

<Text>The food is authentic Mexican food. The menu has a huge selection so there is something for everyone. The food comes out in a timely manner, is well plated so it looks as good as it smells, and it's delicious. The restaurant itself as well as the bathrooms are clean. The staff is friendly and attentive.  The food is so good we haven't been able to take a picture before we start digging in. üòÇ
So far our family has been there twice and we have yet to be disappointed in anything that we've ordered. We try to order something new each time. We've eaten the following during these visits:
üîπBurritos: al pastor, de pollo
Th al pastor was amazing with chunks of pineapple in the burrito. Chicken is well seasoned and not dry.
üîπTacos: pollo,asada,carnitas,mole, pipi√°n
Chicken was well seasoned. Asada was good, hard to compete with the others. Carnitas was amazing. Mole had the flavors just right with enough sauce. Pipi√°n was almost perfect, but it felt a little dry, maybe needed more sauce.
üîπTortas: milanesa de res, milanesa de pollo
The tortas are our favorite so far. The meat is seasoned and breaded perfectly. The amount of chipotle gives it the perfect kick while the avocado complements it. The bread is toasted just right. It all comes together. üòã
üîπEmpanadas: de queso, de tinga
All the toppings complete the crispiness of the outside and the gooey delicious cheese or alternative filling.
üîπChile relleno combination plate with rice and beans
I love chile rellenos, they're my comfort food so I had to try them here and I wasn't disappointed. The rice could use a little work it just doesn't taste like arroz rojo.
The tortillas for the tacos are homemade, not sure about the burrito ones. My 3 year old twins devoured the chicken burrito, chicken tacos, asada taco, and carnitas taco. They also took bites of everything else so I would say all their food is kid friendly and it's not necessary to just order from the kids menu for little ones even though there is one available.
You should definitely try The Taco Shop.
I know we'll keep going back to try to conquer the rest of the menu and to taste their frapp√©s. The Gansito one sounds like it could take me back to my childhood.<//Text>< Pics>

< text>
Spread out in many small campuses, so make sure you are headed for the right campus / building location. Reception is usually not that crowded, and requires an identity card if you are a visitor. You can ask the receptionist to inform your host. Parking is not that crowded. The office locations are in the busy part of the city, so plan your commute accordingly. Also not much eating options inside the campus - but outside you can find something nearby. Quite old company, interesting history - you can read about it while waiting at the reception area.</text>
